name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Twin Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:5 Reviews
rating:2
posted:Posted March 27, 2024
msg:Overall, it is very average. The management and service are the worst among the hotels I have stayed in recently. Let me talk about it in detail. There are two good points: First, the front desk is considerate. They will ask if you need more room cards and solve the problem. The only service points are for the front desk. Second, the hygiene is not bad. There are no obvious omissions. The room is clean and tidy. Other aspects are almost full of complaints: 1. The quality of the air conditioner is very poor, the noise is loud and the cooling effect is particularly poor. The room is stuffy and the body feels particularly bad. 2. The sound insulation is very poor. It seems that there are people dancing square dances, drinking, playing finger-guessing games, and quarreling in the middle of the night outside? And you can hear the conversation and TV in the next room, and you are disturbed by all kinds of noise when you sleep, which is very annoying
3. For a hotel of this size, there are shared equipment in the room. The service quality is really not good
4. Most of the facilities are very old, and the cabinets, toilets, and electrical appliances are old
5. The hotel supplies are not well selected and well maintained. The comfort of the bedding is average. Although the towels absorb water quickly, they feel rough. The toothbrush and paper will also shed hair
6. There is only one public washing machine, which is placed in the public area. It is not convenient to operate and the laundry is very unfriendly
7. When washing clothes, it is found that the sewer pipe is leaking and bubbles will seep out
In general, it feels that the cost saving is too much. Many things can be saved as much as possible, and they can be made up as much as possible. The hotel itself is a service industry. You can't save a few dollars in these aspects, and it will greatly affect the accommodation experience. Why bother?
I usually don't bother to take pictures when I stay in a hotel. This is the first time I have found so many slots and I am so angry. Hahaha
